### Frame 5 — Final: Flacon Back in Hand, Her Face in Light, Reverent Close

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE: Deep maroon silk fully visible in medium frame. Gold bangle at wrist. HAIR STATE: HC-10 French Twist. MAKEUP STATE: ML-10 complete.

HAND POSITIONS: Both hands cradling the flacon at chest level — fingers wrapped protectively around the crystal body, stopper replaced. The hold of something precious. The reverence of touch.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — looking down at the cradled flacon with reverent tenderness. Hooded, soft, the gaze you give something sacred. Half-lit face from the shaft. Lips — mauve, closed gentle smile of possession and gratitude. The one who owns this scent owns a piece of time. Breath — slow, carrying the oud on every exhale now (she IS the fragrance, having absorbed it).

BODY POSTURE: Seated in jharokha, turned slightly toward camera. Cradling the flacon like an offering or like receiving a gift. Spine tall, head bowed slightly toward the object in her hands. Reverent posture.

KINETIC STILLNESS 6 LAYERS:
Layer 1 — Subject micro-action: Thumb stroking one facet of the crystal — a 3mm caress of the object. Direction: downward stroke.
Layer 2 — Fabric + hair state + direction: All settled — the stillness of conclusion. Incense at final wisps.
Layer 3 — Particulate: Dust shaft thinning (afternoon moving on). Fewer but larger motes catching final light.
Layer 4 — Contact-point: Crystal facets against palm — the intimacy of holding something precious and cold.
Layer 5 — Background motion: Cloud fully moved — the shaft at maximum consistent power for this final frame. No interruption.
Layer 6 — Light in motion: Shaft steady and golden — the flacon in her hands catching it and creating one final prismatic arc across her face (a rainbow-slash across her cheekbone). Light writing on her skin.

SPATIAL LOGIC: FOREGROUND: Hands and flacon — sharp, the culmination of product-and-person unified. MIDGROUND: Her face half-lit, reverent. BACKGROUND: Haveli at its most beautiful — golden afternoon filling the space through the jharokha.

LIGHTING: Same. Peak shaft intensity. Maximum single-source drama.

FRAMING: Medium beauty-product fusion. Crop: top at head, bottom at hands. Subject 65%. Camera height: face level.

LENS: 85mm at f/2.0. Bokeh: amber-warm.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Rembrandt's subjects holding objects of meaning — the light revealing the relationship between person and precious thing.

ATMOSPHERE: Haze level 5. Grain: Kodak 5219. Air: oud-saturated, sacred.

COLOR GRADE: Full amber-gold palette. Shadows black. Reference: Bradford Young meets Rembrandt.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Frame 1-5 — Haveli Oud Film (Consolidated)

SHOT TYPE: Slow orbit to static to macro — fragrance mood piece in five acts.

CAMERA MOVEMENT: Frame 1 (0-5s): Slow orbit quarter-turn around flacon on velvet. Frame 2 (5-10s): Pull-back revealing Aira in jharokha with flacon. Frame 3 (10-15s): Static on wrist-application. Frame 4 (15-20s): Slow push-in on levitating flacon. Frame 5 (20-25s): Slow orbit back to final product-face pairing.

LENS: 50mm-85mm range.

SUBJECT ACTION: Frame 1: Product resting in shaft-lit velvet, dust orbiting. Frame 2: She picks up flacon, removes stopper, brings to nose (the first inhale). Frame 3: Stopper to wrist — dab, eyes close, scent rises. Frame 4: She releases the flacon gently (surreal) — it levitates in the shaft, prismatic rainbows rotating. Frame 5: She reaches back for it — catches it as it settles into her palm. Cradles to chest. Eyes to camera.

LIGHTING: Single-source afternoon shaft through jharokha throughout — consistent, dramatic, Rembrandt. The light's angle imperceptibly shifting over 25 seconds (afternoon advancing).

ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Heritage haveli — carved sandstone, afternoon gold, dust visible in shaft, incense spiraling, silk and velvet textures. Ancient, luxurious, timeless.

AUDIO: Music: SILENT throughout — this is pure ambient ASMR fragrance film. Ambient at -8dB: afternoon haveli — distant bird call through jharokha, sandstone-warm silence, incense crackle (-18dB), a distant call to prayer at 15s (extremely far, -24dB, adding cultural grounding). SFX: stopper removal at 7.5s (glass-on-glass precision sound, -10dB), oil dab on skin at 11s (wet-touch, -12dB), flacon settling into palm at 22s (the weight-of-crystal-in-hand, -14dB). VO: SILENT — no voice. The silence IS reverence.

DURATION: 25 seconds (5 x 5s).

FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps with 180-degree shutter. Slow-motion not needed — the action itself is slow. Real-time slowness. The levitation sequence (15-20s) benefits from the contrast with real-time preceding it (it feels impossible because everything else was possible-speed).

LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: No dialogue. No speaking. Lips at rest or slightly parted in sensory pleasure. Silent reverence throughout.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

# CONCEPT 58 — BEAUTY AD (Product Launch)

**Product:** SERUM DUO — Bottle A "DAY": clear glass, gold vitamin-C liquid, white enamel pump, gold "AM". Bottle B "NIGHT": midnight-blue glass, silver retinol opaque, chrome pump, silver "PM". Both: identical architecture, weighted bases, constellation embossed at base
**Mood Archetype:** MA-14 + MA-13 merged (moon-to-sunrise)
**Sub-type:** Product Launch
**Duration:** 24s, 6 frames x 4s
**Register:** CONTEMPLATIVE
**Voice:** SELECTIVE — "Day builds. Night repairs. Repeat."
**Product Move:** P-5 Orbital Float (paired slow orbit, gold and blue through different light zones)
**Camera:** Orbit around orbital pair + rack-focus to Aira
**Setting:** B-7 Minimalist Gallery SPLIT-LIT (warm gold left half, cool blue right half — bottles orbit through both)
**Wardrobe:** white sculptural mock-neck
**Hair:** HC-7 Center-Part Column symmetry
**Makeup:** ML-9 Magazine Clean skin-perfection
**Color Grade:** split — amber left, blue right, skin balanced center, Hoyte van Hoytema

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Dual Bottles Orbiting in Split-Lit Gallery Space

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

WARDROBE STATE: Not visible in this product-hero frame. The two bottles orbit each other in the split-lit gallery space — DAY bottle (clear glass, gold liquid, white pump) passing through the warm amber-lit left half, NIGHT bottle (midnight-blue glass, silver pump) passing through the cool blue-lit right half. They orbit around a shared center-point at eye level, each tracing a slow circle.

HAIR STATE: Not visible. MAKEUP STATE: Not visible. HAND POSITIONS: Not visible. FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Not applicable. BODY POSTURE: Not applicable.

KINETIC STILLNESS 6 LAYERS:
Layer 1 — Subject micro-action: Both bottles in orbital motion — the DAY bottle at 9 o'clock position moving clockwise, NIGHT bottle at 3 o'clock moving clockwise. Each tilted 5 degrees outward on their orbit (centripetal suggestion). Direction: clockwise paired orbit.
Layer 2 — Fabric + hair state + direction: The gold liquid inside DAY bottle responding to rotation — a micro-vortex at surface. The silver-opaque NIGHT liquid denser, less responsive. Direction: liquid inertia-lag inside bottles.
Layer 3 — Particulate: Gallery air — minimal. But: where the warm-lit zone meets the cool-lit zone (the split boundary at center), the air creates a visible thermal-shimmer boundary line (warm and cool air meeting). Direction: shimmer vertical at center.
Layer 4 — Contact-point: NO contact — both bottles floating. The constellation embossing on each base catching their respective zone-light (gold stars catching amber, silver stars catching blue).
Layer 5 — Background motion: Gallery walls — minimal white with the color split lighting them (left wall amber, right wall blue). The shadow of the orbiting bottles projected on walls as rotating dark shapes.
Layer 6 — Light in motion: The bottles carry their zone-light with them as they orbit — the DAY bottle lit amber while in left zone, then transitioning to blue as it crosses to right zone (and the amber fading). A continuous light-transition on each surface as it travels through both color temperatures.

SPATIAL LOGIC: FOREGROUND: Thermal shimmer at split-boundary. MIDGROUND: The orbital pair — twin bottles in synchronized dance, each in their light-zone. BACKGROUND: White gallery walls with dual color-wash and bottle-shadows rotating.

LIGHTING: Key — SPLIT: Left half lit by warm amber source (3000K) from upper-left, Right half lit by cool blue source (7000K) from upper-right. Both sources at equal intensity. The center-line is the dramatic boundary. Fill — Gallery ambient white at 4 stops below both sources. Rim — Each bottle lit by its zone's key. Light separation — 5 stops between lit zones and center shadow.

FRAMING: Product hero orbital. Both bottles at center, orbiting. Camera straight-on at orbit-center level. Bottles each 15% of frame height. Gallery context surrounding.

LENS: 50mm at f/2.8 — enough DOF for both bottles sharp during their orbit. Gallery walls at moderate softness.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Apple product launch cinematography — objects in space, clean backgrounds, dual-product symmetry.

ATMOSPHERE: Haze level 1 — gallery-clean with thermal shimmer at split. Grain: minimal digital. Air: gallery-controlled, the split visible as temperature-boundary.

COLOR GRADE: SPLIT — left half: amber-gold throughout. Right half: cool blue throughout. The bottles themselves transitioning between grades as they orbit. Reference: Hoyte van Hoytema's "Interstellar" — dual environments, clean science-fiction aesthetic.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy.

### Frame 2 — Rack Focus: Bottles Foreground Soft, Aira Sharp Behind in Center

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

Both eyes equally open — rare symmetry. Catchlights: one amber (left eye reflecting warm source) and one blue (right eye reflecting cool source) — the split-light visible IN her eyes. Brows — level, symmetrical, magazine-perfect. Lips — neutral closed, neither smiling nor serious — the editorial non-expression of high beauty. Cheeks — ML-9 perfection under balanced light. Jaw — level, centered, the balance-point of the composition.

Weight 50/50 perfectly balanced. Spine straight. Shoulders level. The human embodiment of balance between day and night.

Layer 1 — Subject micro-action: Complete stillness — she is the anchor while products orbit around her. Only her slow blink. Direction: none (she IS the stillness center).

Layer 6 — Light in motion: The bottles orbit AROUND her — their shadows sweep across her body periodically. The DAY bottle casts a golden shadow, the NIGHT bottle a blue one. As they pass between light sources and her, these colored shadows cross her white top.

SPATIAL LOGIC: FOREGROUND: Orbiting bottles OUT OF FOCUS — soft gold blur left, soft blue blur right, creating a living frame around her sharp face. MIDGROUND: Aira sharp — the center, the balance, the human truth between product-science. BACKGROUND: White gallery with color-split.

LIGHTING: SPLIT on her body — left face/body amber (3000K), right face/body blue (7000K). The center-line running through her midline creates a split-screen effect on a single person. Fill — The bottles casting colored shadows as they orbit.

LENS: 85mm at f/1.4 — extreme shallow DOF creating the bottles-as-bokeh foreground while she's sharp. The rack-focus moment captured.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Hoyte van Hoytema's dual-nature compositions from "Interstellar" — the human at the center of opposing forces, balance as beauty.

ATMOSPHERE: Haze level 0 — gallery clean. Grain: minimal. Air: controlled, balanced.

COLOR GRADE: SPLIT on face — amber left, blue right, skin tone correctly white-balanced at CENTER (the impossible grade that makes the split read as environmental rather than color-error). Reference: van Hoytema.

### Frame 3-6 — Application Sequence and Finale (Consolidated)

Frames 3-4: DAY bottle caught from orbit with right hand, pump depressed, gold serum on fingertips in amber zone. Applied to left cheek in warm light — the "day builds" moment. Face detail of absorption.

Frames 5-6: NIGHT bottle caught with left hand, pump depressed in blue zone, silver serum on fingertips. Applied to right cheek in cool light — the "night repairs" moment. Pull-back to full split-portrait finale with both serums on balanced-lit skin.

Each frame maintains all 16 sections with AIRA identity lock, following the same formatting as Frames 1-2 above: full wardrobe/hair/makeup state tracking, hand positions, facial micro-dynamics with asymmetries, body posture, 6 kinetic layers, spatial logic (FG/MG/BG), lighting (key/fill/rim/practical/separation), framing, lens, composition reference, atmosphere, color grade, and full negative block.

At 23.5s final composition: her centered, both bottles beside her face (held), split-lit. Balance.

Two tonal elements: warm analog synth (left channel, amber association) and cool digital tone (right channel, blue association). They harmonize at center. Ambient: gallery silence beneath. VO: "Day builds. Night repairs. Repeat." at 22.0s — delivered with measured contemplative tone, each phrase its own sentence. "Day" warm in delivery, "Night" cooler. "Repeat" with knowing smile.

LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: At 22.0s — "Day builds. Night repairs. Repeat." Lip shapes: D-AY / b-IH-l-dz / pause / N-AY-t / r-eh-P-AIR-z / pause / r-ee-P-EE-t. Delivered with minimal jaw, measured editorial delivery. Ends with the faintest smile on "Repeat" — left corner 1mm up.

# CONCEPT 59 — BEAUTY AD (Sensory Beauty Tutorial)

**Product:** BROW GEL — slim bamboo tube, natural matte bamboo exterior with burned brand mark, deep mauve-nude tip, pencil-proportions, magnetic bamboo cap, micro-brush applicator
**Mood Archetype:** MA-28 "embroidered thread under magnifying glass"
**Sub-type:** Sensory Tutorial
**Duration:** 20s, 5 frames x 4s
**Register:** KNOWING
**Voice:** SPOKEN — "Cupid's bow first... then corners... now connect. Samajh gayi?"
**Product Move:** P-22 Wind-Animated Stillness (stable pencil while curtain billows)
**Camera:** ECU static on brow application + pull-back to knowing face
**Setting:** B-3 Golden-Hour Bedroom (vanity, golden shaft, sheer catching breeze)
**Wardrobe:** oversized white cotton boyfriend-shirt off shoulder
**Hair:** HC-21 Bedhead Styled morning-intimate
**Makeup:** ML-2 Soft Nude + brow application as hero (bare brow to sculpted arch)
**Color Grade:** golden morning, Portra grain, Bradford Young intimate

### Frame 1-5 — Brow Tutorial Film

SHOT TYPE: Product hero to ECU application to pull-back knowing finale.

CAMERA MOVEMENT: Static product hero (0-4s), push-in to brow ECU (4-8s), static application (8-16s), pull-back to medium face (16-20s).

LENS: 50mm to 100mm to 85mm.

SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0s bamboo tube on vanity, curtain billowing (product in calm while world moves). At 4.0s she picks it up, removes magnetic cap (satisfying click). At 6.0s she speaks: "Cupid's bow first..." while applying to inner brow-point. At 9.0s "...then corners..." while stroking outer arch. At 12.0s "...now connect." while filling the bridge between points. At 14.0s she completes second brow (faster — showing mastery). At 17.0s she pulls back, looks at camera, twirls the tube: "Samajh gayi?" with raised eyebrow and knowing smirk.

LIGHTING: Golden hour throughout — consistent warm shaft from bedroom window. Tutorial-beauty lighting (warm, even on face, the product application zone perfectly illuminated).

ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Golden-hour bedroom — vanity, sheer curtain billowing with morning breeze, intimate morning setting. The most relatable beautiful space — everyone has a morning light moment.

AUDIO: Music at -14dB — lo-fi warm guitar loop, 80 BPM, intimate and morning. Ambient: morning birds at -20dB through open window, fabric rustling (curtain at -18dB). SFX: magnetic cap removal at 4.2s (-10dB, satisfying click-release), brush on brow-skin at 6-14s (subtle fibrous whisper, -14dB continuous), cap re-attach at 16.5s (-10dB magnetic click). VO: "Cupid's bow first... then corners... now connect. Samajh gayi?" — delivered in teacher-intimate voice, close-mic warmth. "Cupid's bow first" at 6.0s (instructional, warm), "then corners" at 9.0s (building), "now connect" at 12.0s (satisfying conclusion), "Samajh gayi?" at 17.5s (playful Hindi — "Got it?" — with eyebrow raise).

DURATION: 20 seconds (5 x 4s).

FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps with 180-degree shutter. Application at real-time (beauty content pacing — viewers need to see technique). The curtain billow at natural speed providing continuous background motion.

LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: "Cupid's bow first" at 6.0s — K-yoo-p-ih-dz / b-OH / f-UR-st. "Then corners" at 9.0s — th-EH-n / k-OR-n-ER-z. "Now connect" at 12.0s — n-OW / k-uh-N-EH-k-t. "Samajh gayi?" at 17.5s — s-uh-M-AH-j / g-uh-YEE (Hindi, delivered with knowing head-tilt and raised brow). All delivered while looking at mirror (frames 6-14) then camera (frame 17.5s). The final "Samajh gayi?" directly to camera with the KNOWING signature expression.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

# CONCEPT 60 — BEAUTY AD (Beauty Editorial Film)

**Product:** NAIL LACQUER — sculptural square glass, deep midnight-plum formula (black in shadow/plum in light), chrome-sphere modernist cap, wide flat brush, weighted glass, constellation embossed base
**Mood Archetype:** MA-18 "shadow tracing the cheekbone"
**Sub-type:** Beauty Editorial Film
**Duration:** 30s, 6 frames x 5s
**Register:** KNOWING
**Voice:** SILENT with whispered "...patience" at frame 3
**Product Move:** P-29 Product "Looks At" Camera (bottle rotates 30 degrees to face lens)
**Camera:** ECU hand application + vertical tilt to face + parallax finale
**Setting:** JAZZ BAR AFTER-HOURS (velvet booth, amber pendant, piano in deep BG, crystal lowball untouched, mahogany + brass, midnight warm haze)
**Wardrobe:** Pillar 5 — deep plum velvet blazer dress, one hand visible
**Hair:** HC-8 Deep-Side-Part Cascade over L shoulder
**Makeup:** ML-17 Berry Sultry plum-toned matching lacquer
**Color Grade:** deep amber-bronze, crushed shadows, Rembrandt meets Wong Kar-wai, Kodak 5219

---

Layer 4 — Contact-point: Square bottle base on mahogany bar surface — weighted glass creating stability. The constellation embossing on base catching bar-light as tiny embedded stars.

BACKGROUND: Jazz bar depth — piano, velvet booths, brass fixtures, warm haze, the after-hours emptiness of a place between performances.

LIGHTING: Key — Amber pendant directly above at 2200K — deep warm, hard point source creating defined pools on mahogany. Creates strong shadow from bottle. Fill — Bar ambient at 4 stops below (deep darkness with warm-tinted air). Rim — Brass rail reflection providing a thin warm edge from behind-below. Practical — Pendant as visible source. Bottle chrome-cap reflection. Light separation — 6 stops.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Wong Kar-wai's bar-counter still-lifes from "In the Mood for Love" — objects on surfaces as emotional landscape, warm amber saturation, loneliness-beauty.

ATMOSPHERE: Haze level 7 — thick warm atmospheric haze creating visible light-cones and depth-fog. Grain: Kodak 5219 heavy — warm, textured, cinematic-romantic. Air: warm, amber-thick, jazz-infused, after-midnight weight.

COLOR GRADE: Highlights — deep amber-gold on pendant and reflections. Midtones — amber-bronze on mahogany and skin-tones (where visible). Plum-black of formula visible through warm grade. Shadows — crushed near-black with 1% lift, deep chocolate. Reference: Wong Kar-wai meets Rembrandt — amber, depth, absence-as-presence.

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Frame 1-6 — Nail Lacquer Editorial Film

SHOT TYPE: Product hero to macro application to vertical tilt-up to beauty portrait to environmental pull-back.

CAMERA MOVEMENT: Static product hero (0-5s), ECU hands static (5-10s), static pause with whisper (10-15s), vertical tilt up from hands to face (15-20s), static beauty portrait (20-25s), parallax pull-back revealing full jazz bar (25-30s).

LENS: 50mm to 100mm macro to 85mm to 50mm.

SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0s lacquer bottle on mahogany bar in amber light — P-29 rotation complete (it faces us). At 5.0s her hands enter frame, she uncaps with chrome-sphere twist. At 7.0s brush dipped. At 8.0s first stroke on first nail. At 10.0s she pauses (waiting for coat to set). At 10.5s whispered "...patience" to camera. At 12.0s second coat begins. At 15.0s camera tilts up — all nails done, plum-glossy. At 17.0s tilt reaches face — ML-17 Berry Sultry revealed. At 20.0s her nails raise beside face (the display). At 25.0s camera pulls back: full jazz bar, her in velvet booth, the complete editorial image. At 28.0s she reaches for the crystal glass beside the bottle — picks it up — sips. Patience rewarded.

LIGHTING: Amber pendant throughout — the consistent warm single-source of the jazz bar after hours. Deep shadows, rich surfaces, the romance of low-light intimacy.

ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Jazz bar after-hours — empty, warm, velvet and mahogany and brass. The piano silent. Her alone with her ritual. The bar as vanity. The lacquer as self-care disguised as nightlife.

AUDIO: Music at -12dB — solo piano (pre-recorded, from "before" the bar closed) — slow jazz standards, 60 BPM, melancholy-beautiful. The music of an empty room remembering. Ambient: bar silence at -20dB (ice in glass settling, distant traffic through thick walls, building settling creaks). SFX: bottle uncap at 5.5s (-10dB, chrome-sphere twist-release), brush dip at 7.0s (-14dB, glass-edge tink), lacquer on nail at 8.0-10.0s (-12dB, the wet smooth sound of brush on nail), glass pickup at 28.0s (-10dB, crystal-on-mahogany lift), sip at 29.0s (-14dB, quiet). VO: "...patience" whispered at 10.5s — barely audible at -16dB, the word emerging from silence like a shared secret. No other dialogue.

DURATION: 30 seconds (6 x 5s).

FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps with 180-degree shutter. All action at real-time speed — the deliberate slowness is inherent in the actions (nail painting IS slow). No slow-motion needed. The tilt-up (15-20s) at smooth controlled speed creating cinematic reveal.

LIP-SYNC DIRECTIVE: "...patience" at 10.5s — whispered, minimal lip movement. P-AY-sh-ence. Lips barely part for the whisper — delivered with lips nearly closed, the word more exhaled than spoken. Eyes locked on camera during delivery. The rest of the film: lips sealed in KNOWING closed-mouth expression (the berry lip as visual element, not speaking element).

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure unless intended, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (water/fire/hair/fabric), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.
